ALAt4	na1[e] + ala_L[e] 	->	na1[c] + ala_L[c] 
ASNt4	na1[e] + asn_L[e] 	->	na1[c] + asn_L[c] 
ASPDt6	h[e] + 3 na1[e] + asp_D[e] + k[c] 	->	h[c] + 3 na1[c] + asp_D[c] + k[e] 
ASPt6	h[e] + 3 na1[e] + k[c] + asp_L[e] 	->	h[c] + 3 na1[c] + asp_L[c] + k[e] 
CREATt4_2_r	2 na1[e] + creat[e] 	<=>	2 na1[c] + creat[c] 
CRNtuNa	na1[e] + crn[e] 	->	na1[c] + crn[c] 
CYSt4	na1[e] + cys_L[e] 	->	na1[c] + cys_L[c] 
FATP3t	na1[c] + ocdca[c] 	<=>	na1[e] + ocdca[e] 
FATP4t	na1[c] + arach[c] 	<=>	na1[e] + arach[e] 
GLUt6	h[e] + 3 na1[e] + k[c] + glu_L[e] 	->	h[c] + 3 na1[c] + glu_L[c] + k[e] 
GLYt4	na1[e] + gly[e] 	->	na1[c] + gly[c] 
HISt4	na1[e] + his_L[e] 	->	na1[c] + his_L[c] 
METt4	na1[e] + met_L[e] 	->	na1[c] + met_L[c] 
NaKt	h2o[c] + atp[c] + na1[c] + k[e] 	->	h[c] + adp[c] + pi[c] + na1[e] + k[c] 
NCKt	4 na1[c] + k[e] + ca2[e] 	<=>	4 na1[e] + k[c] + ca2[c] 
NKCC2t	na1[e] + nh4[e] + 2 cl[e] 	<=>	nh4[c] + na1[c] + 2 cl[c] 
NKCCt	na1[e] + k[e] + 2 cl[e] 	<=>	na1[c] + k[c] + 2 cl[c] 
PHEt4	na1[e] + phe_L[e] 	->	na1[c] + phe_L[c]
